Appearance

From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia

This is a **list of TCP and UDP port numbers** used by protocols for operation of network applications. The [Transmission Control Protocol](/wiki/Transmission_Control_Protocol "Transmission Control Protocol") (TCP) and the [User Datagram Protocol](/wiki/User_Datagram_Protocol "User Datagram Protocol") (UDP) only need one [port](/wiki/Port_\(computer_networking\) "Port (computer networking)") for [bidirectional](/wiki/Duplex_\(telecommunications\) "Duplex (telecommunications)") traffic. TCP usually uses port numbers that match the services of the corresponding UDP implementations, if they exist, and vice versa.

The [Internet Assigned Numbers Authority](/wiki/Internet_Assigned_Numbers_Authority "Internet Assigned Numbers Authority") (IANA) is responsible for maintaining the official assignments of port numbers for specific uses.[\[1\]](#cite_note-1) However, many unofficial uses of both well-known and registered port numbers occur in practice. Similarly, many of the official assignments refer to protocols that were never or are no longer in common use. This article lists port numbers and their associated protocols that have experienced significant uptake.

## Table legend

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=List_of_TCP_and_UDP_port_numbers&action=edit&section=1 "Edit section: Table legend")\]

Legend of TCP and UDP table cells for port numbers

Cell

Description

Yes

Described protocol _is_ assigned this port by IANA, and it _is_: standardized, specified, or widely used on the port.

Unofficial

Described protocol _is not_ assigned this port by IANA, but it _is_: standardized, specified, or widely used on the port.

Assigned

Described protocol _is_ assigned this port by IANA,[\[2\]](#cite_note-IANA-2) but _is not_: standardized, specified, or widely used on the port.

No

Described protocol _is not_ assigned this port by IANA or standardized, specified, or widely used on the port.

Reserved

Port is reserved by IANA,[\[2\]](#cite_note-IANA-2) generally to prevent collision after its previous assignment was withdrawn.[\[3\]](#cite_note-rfc6335-3)[\[4\]](#cite_note-4) The port number may be available for assignment upon request to IANA.[\[3\]](#cite_note-rfc6335-3)

## Well-known ports

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=List_of_TCP_and_UDP_port_numbers&action=edit&section=2 "Edit section: Well-known ports")\]

This is a [dynamic list](/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Lists#Dynamic_lists "Wikipedia:WikiProject Lists") and may never be able to satisfy particular standards for completeness. You can help by [editing the page](/wiki/Special:EditPage/List_of_TCP_and_UDP_port_numbers "Special:EditPage/List of TCP and UDP port numbers") to add missing items, with references to [reliable sources](/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources "Wikipedia:Reliable sources").

The port numbers in the range from 0 to 1023 (0 to 210 − 1) are the _well-known ports_ or _system ports_.[\[3\]](#cite_note-rfc6335-3) They are used by system processes that provide widely used types of network services. On [Unix-like](/wiki/Unix-like "Unix-like") operating systems, a process must execute with [superuser](/wiki/Superuser "Superuser") privileges to be able to bind a [network socket](/wiki/Network_socket "Network socket") to an [IP address](/wiki/IP_address "IP address") using one of the well-known ports.[\[5\]](#cite_note-5)

[TCP](/wiki/Transmission_Control_Protocol "Transmission Control Protocol")

[UDP](/wiki/User_Datagram_Protocol "User Datagram Protocol")

[SCTP](/wiki/Stream_Control_Transmission_Protocol "Stream Control Transmission Protocol")

[DCCP](/wiki/Datagram_Congestion_Control_Protocol "Datagram Congestion Control Protocol")

Description

0

Reserved

In programming APIs (not in communication between hosts), requests a system-allocated (dynamic) port[\[6\]](#cite_note-6)

Yes

Assigned

[TCP Port Service Multiplexer](/wiki/TCP_Port_Service_Multiplexer "TCP Port Service Multiplexer") (TCPMUX). Historic. Both TCP and UDP have been assigned to TCPMUX by IANA,[\[2\]](#cite_note-IANA-2) but by design only TCP is specified.[\[7\]](#cite_note-7)

2

Reserved

De-assigned on 2025-02-13, previously compressnet[\[2\]](#cite_note-IANA-2)

3

Reserved

De-assigned on 2025-02-13, previously compressnet[\[2\]](#cite_note-IANA-2)

5

Assigned

[Remote Job Entry](/wiki/Remote_Job_Entry "Remote Job Entry")[\[8\]](#cite_note-8) was historically using socket 5 in its [old socket form](/wiki/Network_socket#History "Network socket"), while [MIB](/wiki/Management_information_base "Management information base") [PIM](/wiki/Protocol_Independent_Multicast "Protocol Independent Multicast") has identified it as TCP/5[\[9\]](#cite_note-9) and IANA has assigned both TCP and UDP 5 to it.

## Registered ports

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=List_of_TCP_and_UDP_port_numbers&action=edit&section=3 "Edit section: Registered ports")\]

This is a [dynamic list](/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Lists#Dynamic_lists "Wikipedia:WikiProject Lists") and may never be able to satisfy particular standards for completeness. You can help by [editing the page](/wiki/Special:EditPage/List_of_TCP_and_UDP_port_numbers "Special:EditPage/List of TCP and UDP port numbers") to add missing items, with references to [reliable sources](/wiki/Wikipedia:Reliable_sources "Wikipedia:Reliable sources").

The range of port numbers from 1024 to 49151 (210 to 215 + 214 − 1) are the [registered ports](/wiki/Registered_port "Registered port"). They are assigned by [IANA](/wiki/Internet_Assigned_Numbers_Authority "Internet Assigned Numbers Authority") for specific service upon application by a requesting entity.[\[2\]](#cite_note-IANA-2) On most systems, registered ports can be used without superuser privileges.

## Dynamic, private or ephemeral ports

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=List_of_TCP_and_UDP_port_numbers&action=edit&section=4 "Edit section: Dynamic, private or ephemeral ports")\]

See also: [Ephemeral port](/wiki/Ephemeral_port "Ephemeral port")

The range 49152–65535 (215 + 214 to 216 − 1), 16 384 ports, contains dynamic or private ports that cannot be registered with IANA.[\[509\]](#cite_note-511) This range is used for private or customized services, for temporary purposes, and for automatic allocation of [ephemeral ports](/wiki/Ephemeral_port "Ephemeral port").

Dynamic, private or ephemeral ports

TCP

UDP

SCTP

DCCP

Description

## Note

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=List_of_TCP_and_UDP_port_numbers&action=edit&section=5 "Edit section: Note")\]

1.  **[^](#cite_ref-tcp465_93-0)** TCP port 465 was originally assigned to allow the use of [SMTP](/wiki/Simple_Mail_Transfer_Protocol "Simple Mail Transfer Protocol") over [SSL](/wiki/Transport_Layer_Security "Transport Layer Security") ([SMTPS](/wiki/SMTPS "SMTPS")), but practical concerns meant that it was left unused and according to the registration rules at that time was subsequently revoked and eventually re-assigned for use by [Cisco](/wiki/Cisco "Cisco")'s URD protocol. Subsequently, port 587 was assigned as the SMTP submission port, but was initially in [plaintext](/wiki/Plaintext "Plaintext"), with encryption eventually provided years later by the [STARTTLS](/wiki/STARTTLS "STARTTLS") extension. At the same time, the subsequent adoption of the usage of 465 as an SSL-enabled SMTP submission port, even though the original registration did not envision that usage and despite the fact that it was registered to another service has endured. Subsequently, RFC 8314, in a special exemption to the normal assignment process as defined by RFC 6335, acknowledges the _de-facto_ situation and not only designates message submission over implicit TLS as an 'alternate usage assignment' but establishes this as the preferred method and calls for transition away from port 587 and STARTTLS.
2.  **[^](#cite_ref-133)** Deployment typically occurs only directly over UDP, but other underlying protocol layers which meet the requirements described in the specification are possible.

Only the Private Ports 49152-65535 may be used in this manner (without registration). The ports in the range of 1-49151 \[_[sic](/wiki/Sic "Sic")?_\] SHOULD NOT be used. ...

512.  ^ [_**a**_](#cite_ref-s-connect_514-0) [_**b**_](#cite_ref-s-connect_514-1) ["The description of the S-Connect protocol"](https://solarcontrols.cz/en/sconnect.html). _SOLAR controls s.r.o_.
513.  **[^](#cite_ref-515)** ["transmission/docs/Port-Forwarding-Guide.md at main · transmission/transmission · GitHub"](https://github.com/transmission/transmission/blob/main/docs/Port-Forwarding-Guide.md#windows). _GitHub_. 2022-10-13. [Archived](https://web.archive.org/web/20241228123715/https://github.com/transmission/transmission/blob/main/docs/Port-Forwarding-Guide.md#windows) from the original on 2024-12-28. Retrieved 2025-01-02.
514.  **[^](#cite_ref-516)** ["Repository Server"](https://web.archive.org/web/20250211080246/https://kopia.io/docs/repository-server/). 2025-02-11. Archived from [the original](https://kopia.io/docs/repository-server/) on 2025-02-11. Retrieved 2025-02-11.
515.  **[^](#cite_ref-517)** ["Quick Start Guide"](https://www.wireguard.com/quickstart/). _WireGuard_. Retrieved 20 September 2022.
516.  ^ [_**a**_](#cite_ref-visca-over-ip_518-0) [_**b**_](#cite_ref-visca-over-ip_518-1) ["VISCA Command List 2.00 for ILME-FR7"](https://pro.sony/s3/2022/09/14131603/VISCA-Command-List-Version-2.00.pdf) (PDF). Retrieved 13 December 2024.
517.  **[^](#cite_ref-519)** ["GitHub – localsend/localsend: An open-source cross-platform alternative to AirDrop"](https://github.com/localsend/localsend#setup/). _GitHub_. Retrieved 2025-10-13.
518.  **[^](#cite_ref-520)** ["AudioRelay – FAQ"](https://docs.audiorelay.net/faq). Retrieved 17 October 2024.
519.  **[^](#cite_ref-521)** ["Mosh"](https://mosh.org/). mosh.org. Retrieved 2017-07-10.
520.  **[^](#cite_ref-522)** ["ActiveMQ"](https://activemq.apache.org/components/classic/documentation/getting-started).
521.  **[^](#cite_ref-523)** ["Usbmux"](https://www.theiphonewiki.com/wiki/Usbmux#lockdownd_protocol). _The iPhone Wiki_. Retrieved 2024-09-08.
522.  **[^](#cite_ref-524)** ["Mumble Murmur Server default config file – commit 73a0b2f"](https://github.com/mumble-voip/mumble/blob/73a0b2f88812e99ac50a78b22dad53336177e78e/scripts/murmur.ini#L123). _Mumble Source Code Repository_. Github. Retrieved 29 October 2018.\[_[self-published source](/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Self-published_sources "Wikipedia:Verifiability")_\]

-   Stretch, Jeremy. ["Common Ports"](http://packetlife.net/media/library/23/common_ports.pdf) (PDF). _PacketLife.net_. [Archived](https://web.archive.org/web/20180328160447/http://packetlife.net/media/library/23/common_ports.pdf) (PDF) from the original on 2018-03-28. Retrieved 2019-02-09.
